## Locked constraints (do not reopen)

1. Generator = DeepSeek V4 Pro (1.6T MoE); Evaluator = Gemma 4 31B; 1 concurrent session, traffic limited.
2. Canadian sovereign GPU — 8× H200 / 12-16× H100. Not OVH-Canada (no Hopper there), not France, not US. Pursuing Vexxhost + ISAIC.
3. Architecture = deployed v6 stack (redis + api + worker + webui). No rewrites.
4. "BPEI" name banned — rename all 407 files to `ambiguity_detector`.
5. Demo: single venue, PM Carney's office, flexible June 2026 date.

## Honest framing of effort (Codex-corrected)

Two estimate bands, not one:
- **Optimistic:** Claude-side ready ~3.5 weeks; demo achievable second-half June IF the GPU lands early and scope stays locked to the demo path.
- **Conservative:** Claude-side ready ~4-5 weeks; demo late June / very-early July.
- v1's "3 weeks" was an over-claim. Plan against the conservative band; treat optimistic as best-case.

## The plan — phases + one parallel workstream

Legend: **[no GPU]** buildable/prevalidatable without the sovereign GPU (final sovereign gates still close after cutover). **[GPU]** needs the GPU. **[operator]** operator action.

### Phase 0A — Lock constraints **[no GPU]** — ~0.5 day
- Write `docs/polaris_locked_scope.md`: the 5 locked constraints + canonical 8 templates + the 15-feature list. Hash-pin the *constraints* section only.
- **Do NOT pin feature statuses yet** — those are unverified (Codex catch). Mark them "provisional, pending Phase 1."
- **Exit:** constraints frozen.

### Phase 1 — Verify gaps (P0 + schedule-affecting P1) **[no GPU]** — ~2-3 days
- Open the running system; test each gap. Mark CONFIRMED-BROKEN vs WORKS-UNTESTED.
- P0s: UI sign-in, live-run-ID into inspector, worker document_ids, F5-F15 live-vs-fixture.
- **Also verify the P1s that affect schedule** (Codex catch): cancel/resume state, memory durability/isolation, sovereignty + log-redaction call-site wiring, GPG bundle signing, UI hardening states.
- **Exit:** every P0 + schedule-relevant P1 has a verified status.

### Phase 0B — Pin verified statuses **[no GPU]** — ~0.25 day
- After Phase 1, update `docs/polaris_locked_scope.md` with the *verified* per-feature statuses and hash-pin the full doc.
- **Exit:** lock doc reflects grounded reality, fully pinned.

### Phase 2 — Deploy-reconciliation + rename **[no GPU]** — ~1-2 days
- **I-bug-113 deploy PR:** box-vs-repo fixes (langchain pins, bcrypt, CRLF entrypoint, healthchecks, `.gitattributes`). Without this any rebuild wipes the live deploy.
- **BPEI rename:** all 407 files → `ambiguity_detector`; delete legacy `src/polaris_v6/bpei/`. One PR.
- **Exit:** repo == box; zero "BPEI"; CI green.

### Phase 3 — Fix the integration (P0 + the build-not-test P1s) **[no GPU]** — ~12-18 working days
The long pole. Each item a GitHub issue (§3.0 workflow). Codex-expanded scope:
1. **Auth/SSE operability** — real sign-in page; bearer-token injection in the web API client; SSE auth (token via query param or cookie — `EventSource` can't set headers).
2. **Templates → canonical 8** — one source of truth; landing page + TS types + v6 registry all read from `config/scope_templates/`.
3. **Model/config alignment** — purge stale V4 Flash / qwen / GLM; everything → V4 Pro + Gemma; transparency endpoint matches.
4. **Live-run artifact contract** — define the contract that maps a completed run's artifacts to what the inspector, charts, follow-up, compare, **pin replay**, **memory**, and bundle each consume. (Codex: this is the root fix.)
5. **Live-run → rich UI** — inspector, charts, follow-up, compare, **F13 pin replay**, **F14 memory**, bundle all accept a real completed run ID, not only golden fixtures.
6. **ambiguity_detector product wiring** — wire it into the main ask/create-run flow (rename alone does not make F2 product-integrated — Codex catch).
7. **Document grounding** — async worker passes uploaded `document_ids` into the pipeline; F3 works end-to-end.
8. **Cancellation/resume** — implement the disabled UI cancel + the xfailed backend resume (Codex catch — this is build work, not test work).
9. **Durable workspace-scoped memory** — F14 real durability + workspace isolation + cited recall + migration (Codex catch).
10. **1-concurrent-session enforcement** — queue/rejection UX when a second request arrives (Codex catch — required by the locked 1-concurrent constraint).
11. **Assemble the journey** — global nav in `layout.tsx`; coherent path land → template → ask → live audit → integrated report → inspect → follow-up/compare/pin/memory → signed bundle; hide the 17 harness routes.
- **Exit:** the full journey works against a stub LLM, with auth on.

### Workstream L — No-GPU demo logistics (PARALLEL, starts after Phase 2) **[no GPU]**
Runs alongside Phase 3 (Codex catch — don't leave these to the end):
- TLS / HTTPS for `polarisresearch.ca` (Caddy).
- Off-box backup of orchestrator state.
- Legal/privacy notice (PIPEDA / Law 25) — G18.
- T1 source snapshot cache — G8; Serper exception canary — G9.
- Live ops runbook + named runbook owner + demo credentials + monitoring + rollback/teardown rehearsal — G14.
- Fallback laptop drill prep — G5; browser-compatibility test authoring — G10 (browser part).
- GPG signing key readiness + clean-machine bundle-verification criteria.

### Phase 4 — OpenRouter rehearsal **[no GPU, but not dependency-free]** — ~2-3 days
- Wire the LLM endpoint as env vars; point at OpenRouter V4 Pro + Gemma.
- **OpenRouter evidence package (Codex catch):** model-availability check, a fixed non-confidential prompt set, key-removal proof procedure, and an explicit env-diff to the sovereign config.
- Run the full journey end-to-end with the real model; fix what breaks.
- **Exit:** the **non-sovereign rehearsal path** passes start-to-finish. (This proves the product + model; it does NOT prove sovereign topology.)

### Phase 5 — Test matrix (STAGED, Codex-restructured) **[no GPU to author/run; sovereign rerun is GPU]**
- **5a authoring** — write the 22-type matrix against the product journey, *during* Phase 3.
- **5b run** — execute against stub + OpenRouter, *after* Phase 3/4.
- **5c sovereign regression** — rerun the risk-based regression subset *after* Phase 7.
- **Exit:** 5a/5b green pre-cutover; 5c green post-cutover.

### Phase 6 — GPU acquisition **[operator]** — parallel to Phases 0-5, 3-10 day lead
- Vexxhost / ISAIC replies → confirm Canadian physical location + price → pick → provision.
- **Hard decision gate 2026-05-24:** no Canadian H100/H200 → halt-and-decide (non-Canadian / change model / move date).
- **Exit:** a Canadian H100/H200 instance reachable.

### Phase 7 — Sovereign cutover **[GPU]** — ~2-3 days after GPU
- Stand up vLLM serving V4 Pro + Gemma on the Canadian GPU.
- Swap the LLM endpoint env vars OpenRouter → GPU. (Designed as a one-env-change; **verify** — current config uses key/base-url/model gates, not yet proven single-var.)
- **Full sovereign regression (Codex catch — more than a journey rerun):** LLM path, egress lockdown, log-redaction call sites, GPG bundle signing + clean-machine verification, two-family segregation re-verified, OpenRouter key removed + proven removed.
- **Exit:** the full product runs on Canadian sovereign hardware; Phase 5c green.

### Phase 8 — Final demo logistics **[GPU for the live-system parts]** — ~3-4 days
- Full sovereign dress rehearsal — G1.
- Pre-recorded "known-good" fallback runs — G6.
- End-to-end venue rehearsal against the live sovereign system — G10 (live part); capacity + cold-start timing — G11.
- 5 canonical + 5 staff-style rehearsal questions, §-1.1 line-by-line audited — GH#473.
- Audit calibration — G15; handover scope lock — G16; reproducibility claim narrowed to "replayable provenance" — G17.
- **Exit:** dress rehearsal passes; fallback proven; runbook final.

### Phase 9 — Demo + handover
- Carney office demo (I-hand-003); handover package (I-hand-001/002).
- Post-demo: GPU + orchestrator teardown to stop billing; secret rotation (G13 sheet exists).

.codex/carney-execution-plan-review\codex_verdict.txt:1436:19338:The rationale for accepting the exception: POLARIS's sovereignty constraint protects the **LLM inference path and the generated report data** — those run on Canadian/non-US infrastructure (Vexxhost orchestrator + OVH H200 inference). # POLARIS Carney demo — readiness gap register

**Date:** 2026-05-15. **Source:** Claude grounded inventory + Codex independent
gap-analysis consult (`.codex/carney-readiness-gap-analysis/`).
**Codex verdict:** REQUEST_CHANGES — the readiness picture is missing material parts.

---

## The core finding (deeper than "test harness pages")

POLARIS's features were each built as **substrates + test-harness pages + golden
fixtures**, and each GitHub issue was completed *as scoped* and Codex-reviewed.
BUT the **rich product surfaces do not consume live run output** — the inspector,
charts, follow-up, compare, bundle paths are **fixture-bound** (they display
golden test fixtures, not the artifacts a real run produces).

Consequence: even with a working LLM, a real run will produce a run — but
click-through inspection, chart provenance, follow-up, compare, pin replay,
memory, and bundle export **from that same run** are not wired. This is the
`bpei_phantom_completion` pattern: issue-level "done" ≠ product-level "done."

So the GPU-wait window is NOT "testing time." It is **integration time** — and
that work mostly does not need the GPU.

---

## Per-feature honest status (Codex + Claude)

| Feature | Substrate | Product-integrated? |
|---|---|---|
| F1 scope/templates | landing UI exists | template cards don't match canonical templates |
| F2 ambiguity detector | backend + modal exist | not consistently wired into main run flow |
| F3 upload/grounding | upload UI + API exist | only text/markdown parse fully; async runs don't consume uploaded docs |
| F4 live audit SSE | Redis SSE substrate works | run page shows raw event cards, not frontier-grade |
| F5-F9 inspector/hover/coverage/contradiction/two-family | strong components exist | live in `/generation`, fixtures, harness pages — NOT the live `/runs/{id}` report |
| F10 charts | spec builder + API + tests | charts are fixture-bound; harness does the visual coverage |
| F11 follow-up | backend + harness exist | product run page has follow-up DISABLED |
| F12 compare | backend + harness exist | no real product route |
| F13 pin replay | page exists | uses demo data; says production fetch lands later |
| F14 memory | page + API exist | hardcoded demo workspace, in-memory store — not durable cited recall |
| F15 bundle export | tar.gz backend works for live artifacts | inspector JSON bundle path is fixture-only; clean-machine verify not proven |

## P0 — blocks the demo (8)

1. Secure Canadian H100/H200 GPU + full sovereign dress rehearsal. *(in progress — Vexxhost/ISAIC outreach sent)*
2. Make ONE coherent v6 product journey work end-to-end: landing → create run → live audit → integrated report → inspect claims → follow-up/compare/pin/memory → signed bundle.
3. Connect live run outputs to the rich inspector/report/bundle path (today they are fixture-indexed).
4. Fix auth for the deployed UI: sign-in page is a disabled placeholder, the web API client sends no bearer token, and browser `EventSource` can't send auth headers to protected SSE. **With auth enabled (as deployed), the UI cannot operate.**
5. Reconcile templates to the canonical 8 (`clinical, policy, tech, due_diligence, ai_sovereignty, canada_us, workforce, custom`) — currently split across 3-4 conflicting sources.
6. Align model/env/docs/transparency with locked **DeepSeek V4 Pro + Gemma 4 31B** — stale V4 Flash / qwen / GLM references remain.
7. Wire CLIENT document upload/grounding into async runs (the worker actor ignores uploaded `document_ids`).
8. Product-integrate F10-F15 instead of relying on harness/demo-data pages.

## P1 (7)

- Complete cancellation/resume (UI cancel disabled, backend xfailed).
- Make memory durable + workspace-scoped with cited recall.
- Run the full 22-type test matrix against the actual product journey (current coverage is mostly harness/fixture).
- Finish sovereignty + log-redaction CI and prove enforcement at every external call site.
- Signed-bundle clean-machine verification.
- Harden loading/empty/error/network/accessibility/performance states across the real journey.
- Demo logistics: fallback recordings, T-1 laptop drill, venue browser/network test, T1 source cache, PIPEDA/Law25 legal notice.

## P2 (4)

- Polish the visual design system + route consistency.
- Remove scaffold/demo-data copy from user-visible pages.
- Archive/hide the 17 harness pages from demo navigation.
- Clean stale docs/env comments after the lock doc is correct.

## Claude's filter on the Codex verdict

- The findings are **real and well-grounded** — consistent with the phantom-completion pattern and the per-issue-fixture build history.
- Many items are phrased "not evidenced / not proven" — that means *Codex could not find proof it works*, NOT *proven broken*. The P0 list needs a **verification pass first** (some may already work and just lack a product test) before assuming a full rebuild.
- The recommended sequence is sound and matches the operator's "lock scope first" instruction.

## Recommended sequence (Codex, accepted)

1. Write the **truthful lock document** — LLM + architecture + features + the canonical 8 templates + this RED gap list stated openly + the rule "harness/fixture evidence does not count as feature-complete."
2. Verify + fix P0 product connections, in order: auth/SSE → canonical templates → live-run→report/bundle → document grounding → locked model endpoint config.
3. Assemble the one navigable v6 journey; remove scaffold surfaces from the demo path.
4. OpenRouter V4 Pro rehearsal (non-confidential, key removed before demo).
5. Swap unchanged onto the Canadian GPU.
6. Full product-focused test matrix + clean-machine bundle verify + fallback drill + egress validation + venue rehearsal.
